29	    #define _NPY_VERSION_CONCAT_HELPER2(x, y) x ## y
30	    #define _NPY_VERSION_CONCAT_HELPER(arg) \
31	        _NPY_VERSION_CONCAT_HELPER2(arg, PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION)
32	    #define PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION \
33	        _NPY_VERSION_CONCAT_HELPER(PY_ARRAY_UNIQUE_SYMBOL)
34	#endif
35	
36	/* By default do not export API in an .so (was never the case on windows) */
37	#ifndef NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE
38	    #define NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE NPY_VISIBILITY_HIDDEN
39	#endif
40	
41	#if defined(NO_IMPORT) || defined(NO_IMPORT_ARRAY)
42	extern NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE void **PyArray_API;
43	extern NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE int PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION;
44	#else
45	#if defined(PY_ARRAY_UNIQUE_SYMBOL)
46	NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE void **PyArray_API;
47	NPY_API_SYMBOL_ATTRIBUTE int PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION;
48	#else
49	static void **PyArray_API = NULL;
50	static int PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION = 0;
51	#endif
52	#endif
53	
54	%s
55	
56	/*
57	 * The DType classes are inconvenient for the Python generation so exposed
58	 * manually in the header below  (may be moved).
59	 */
60	#include "numpy/_public_dtype_api_table.h"
61	
62	#if !defined(NO_IMPORT_ARRAY) && !defined(NO_IMPORT)
63	static int
64	_import_array(void)
65	{
66	  int st;
67	  PyObject *numpy = PyImport_ImportModule("numpy._core._multiarray_umath");
68	  if (numpy == NULL && PyErr_ExceptionMatches(PyExc_ModuleNotFoundError)) {
69	    PyErr_Clear();
70	    numpy = PyImport_ImportModule("numpy.core._multiarray_umath");
71	  }
72	
73	  if (numpy == NULL) {
74	      return -1;
75	  }
76	
77	  PyObject *c_api = PyObject_GetAttrString(numpy, "_ARRAY_API");
78	  Py_DECREF(numpy);
79	  if (c_api == NULL) {
80	      return -1;
81	  }
82	
83	  if (!PyCapsule_CheckExact(c_api)) {
84	      PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "_ARRAY_API is not PyCapsule object");
85	      Py_DECREF(c_api);
86	      return -1;
87	  }
88	  PyArray_API = (void **)PyCapsule_GetPointer(c_api, NULL);
89	  Py_DECREF(c_api);
90	  if (PyArray_API == NULL) {
91	      PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "_ARRAY_API is NULL pointer");
92	      return -1;
93	  }
94	
95	  /*
96	   * On exceedingly few platforms these sizes may not match, in which case
97	   * We do not support older NumPy versions at all.
98	   */
99	  if (sizeof(Py_ssize_t) != sizeof(Py_intptr_t) &&
100	        PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION < NPY_2_0_API_VERSION) {
101	    PyErr_Format(PyExc_RuntimeError,
102	        "module compiled against NumPy 2.0 but running on NumPy 1.x. "
103	        "Unfortunately, this is not supported on niche platforms where "
104	        "`sizeof(size_t) != sizeof(inptr_t)`.");
105	  }
106	  /*
107	   * Perform runtime check of C API version.  As of now NumPy 2.0 is ABI
108	   * backwards compatible (in the exposed feature subset!) for all practical
109	   * purposes.
110	   */
111	  if (NPY_VERSION < PyArray_GetNDArrayCVersion()) {
112	      PyErr_Format(PyExc_RuntimeError, "module compiled against "\
113	             "ABI version 0x%%x but this version of numpy is 0x%%x", \
114	             (int) NPY_VERSION, (int) PyArray_GetNDArrayCVersion());
115	      return -1;
116	  }
117	  PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION = (int)PyArray_GetNDArrayCFeatureVersion();
118	  if (NPY_FEATURE_VERSION > PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION) {
119	      PyErr_Format(PyExc_RuntimeError,
120	             "module was compiled against NumPy C-API version 0x%%x "
121	             "(NumPy " NPY_FEATURE_VERSION_STRING ") "
122	             "but the running NumPy has C-API version 0x%%x. "
123	             "Check the section C-API incompatibility at the "
124	             "Troubleshooting ImportError section at "
125	             "https://numpy.org/devdocs/user/troubleshooting-importerror.html"
126	             "#c-api-incompatibility "
127	             "for indications on how to solve this problem.",
128	             (int)NPY_FEATURE_VERSION, PyArray_RUNTIME_VERSION);
129	      return -1;
130	  }
131	
132	  /*
133	   * Perform runtime check of endianness and check it matches the one set by
134	   * the headers (npy_endian.h) as a safeguard
135	   */
136	  st = PyArray_GetEndianness();
137	  if (st == NPY_CPU_UNKNOWN_ENDIAN) {
138	      PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError,
139	                      "FATAL: module compiled as unknown endian");
140	      return -1;
141	  }
142	#if NPY_BYTE_ORDER == NPY_BIG_ENDIAN
143	  if (st != NPY_CPU_BIG) {
144	      PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError,
145	                      "FATAL: module compiled as big endian, but "
146	                      "detected different endianness at runtime");
147	      return -1;
148	  }
149	#elif NPY_BYTE_ORDER == NPY_LITTLE_ENDIAN
150	  if (st != NPY_CPU_LITTLE) {
151	      PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError,
152	                      "FATAL: module compiled as little endian, but "
153	                      "detected different endianness at runtime");
154	      return -1;
155	  }
156	#endif
157	
158	  return 0;
159	}
160	
161	#define import_array() { \
162	  if (_import_array() < 0) { \
163	    PyErr_Print(); \
164	    PyErr_SetString( \
165	        PyExc_ImportError, \
166	        "numpy._core.multiarray failed to import" \
167	    ); \
168	    return NULL; \
169	  } \
170	}
171	
172	#define import_array1(ret) { \
173	  if (_import_array() < 0) { \
174	    PyErr_Print(); \
175	    PyErr_SetString( \
176	        PyExc_ImportError, \
177	        "numpy._core.multiarray failed to import" \
178	    ); \
179	    return ret; \
180	  } \
181	}
182	
183	#define import_array2(msg, ret) { \
184	  if (_import_array() < 0) { \
185	    PyErr_Print(); \
186	    PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ImportError, msg); \
187	    return ret; \
188	  } \
189	}
190	
191	#endif
192	
193	#endif
194	"""

49	      f2py -c [<options>, <build_flib options>, <extra options>] <fortran files>
50	
51	3) To generate signature files:
52	
53	      f2py -h <filename.pyf> ...< same options as in (1) >
54	
55	Description: This program generates a Python C/API file (<modulename>module.c)
56	             that contains wrappers for given fortran functions so that they
57	             can be called from Python. With the -c option the corresponding
58	             extension modules are built.
59	
60	Options:
61	
62	  -h <filename>    Write signatures of the fortran routines to file <filename>
63	                   and exit. You can then edit <filename> and use it instead
64	                   of <fortran files>. If <filename>==stdout then the
65	                   signatures are printed to stdout.
66	  <fortran functions>  Names of fortran routines for which Python C/API
67	                   functions will be generated. Default is all that are found
68	                   in <fortran files>.
69	  <fortran files>  Paths to fortran/signature files that will be scanned for
70	                   <fortran functions> in order to determine their signatures.
71	  skip:            Ignore fortran functions that follow until `:'.
72	  only:            Use only fortran functions that follow until `:'.
73	  :                Get back to <fortran files> mode.
74	
75	  -m <modulename>  Name of the module; f2py generates a Python/C API
76	                   file <modulename>module.c or extension module <modulename>.
77	                   Default is 'untitled'.
78	
79	  '-include<header>'  Writes additional headers in the C wrapper, can be passed
80	                      multiple times, generates #include <header> each time.
81	
82	  --[no-]lower     Do [not] lower the cases in <fortran files>. By default,
83	                   --lower is assumed with -h key, and --no-lower without -h key.
84	
85	  --build-dir <dirname>  All f2py generated files are created in <dirname>.
86	                   Default is tempfile.mkdtemp().
87	
88	  --overwrite-signature  Overwrite existing signature file.
89	
90	  --[no-]latex-doc Create (or not) <modulename>module.tex.
91	                   Default is --no-latex-doc.
92	  --short-latex    Create 'incomplete' LaTeX document (without commands
93	                   \\documentclass, \\tableofcontents, and \\begin{{document}},
94	                   \\end{{document}}).
95	
96	  --[no-]rest-doc Create (or not) <modulename>module.rst.
97	                   Default is --no-rest-doc.
98	
99	  --debug-capi     Create C/API code that reports the state of the wrappers
100	                   during runtime. Useful for debugging.
101	
102	  --[no-]wrap-functions    Create Fortran subroutine wrappers to Fortran 77
103	                   functions. --wrap-functions is default because it ensures
104	                   maximum portability/compiler independence.
105	
106	  --[no-]freethreading-compatible    Create a module that declares it does or
107	                   doesn't require the GIL. The default is
108	                   --freethreading-compatible for backward
109	                   compatibility. Inspect the Fortran code you are wrapping for
110	                   thread safety issues before passing
111	                   --no-freethreading-compatible, as f2py does not analyze
112	                   fortran code for thread safety issues.
113	
114	  --include-paths <path1>:<path2>:...   Search include files from the given
115	                   directories.
116	
117	  --help-link [..] List system resources found by system_info.py. See also
118	                   --link-<resource> switch below. [..] is optional list
119	                   of resources names. E.g. try 'f2py --help-link lapack_opt'.
120	
121	  --f2cmap <filename>  Load Fortran-to-Python KIND specification from the given
122	                   file. Default: .f2py_f2cmap in current directory.
123	
124	  --quiet          Run quietly.
125	  --verbose        Run with extra verbosity.
126	  --skip-empty-wrappers   Only generate wrapper files when needed.
127	  -v               Print f2py version ID and exit.
128	
129	
130	build backend options (only effective with -c)
131	[NO_MESON] is used to indicate an option not meant to be used
132	with the meson backend or above Python 3.12:
133	
134	  --fcompiler=         Specify Fortran compiler type by vendor [NO_MESON]
135	  --compiler=          Specify distutils C compiler type [NO_MESON]
136	
137	  --help-fcompiler     List available Fortran compilers and exit [NO_MESON]
138	  --f77exec=           Specify the path to F77 compiler [NO_MESON]
139	  --f90exec=           Specify the path to F90 compiler [NO_MESON]
140	  --f77flags=          Specify F77 compiler flags
141	  --f90flags=          Specify F90 compiler flags
142	  --opt=               Specify optimization flags [NO_MESON]
143	  --arch=              Specify architecture specific optimization flags [NO_MESON]
144	  --noopt              Compile without optimization [NO_MESON]
145	  --noarch             Compile without arch-dependent optimization [NO_MESON]
146	  --debug              Compile with debugging information
147	
148	  --dep                <dependency>
149	                       Specify a meson dependency for the module. This may
150	                       be passed multiple times for multiple dependencies.
151	                       Dependencies are stored in a list for further processing.
152	
153	                       Example: --dep lapack --dep scalapack
154	                       This will identify "lapack" and "scalapack" as dependencies
155	                       and remove them from argv, leaving a dependencies list
156	                       containing ["lapack", "scalapack"].
157	
158	  --backend            <backend_type>
159	                       Specify the build backend for the compilation process.
160	                       The supported backends are 'meson' and 'distutils'.
161	                       If not specified, defaults to 'distutils'. On
162	                       Python 3.12 or higher, the default is 'meson'.
163	
164	Extra options (only effective with -c):
165	
166	  --link-<resource>    Link extension module with <resource> as defined
167	                       by numpy.distutils/system_info.py. E.g. to link
168	                       with optimized LAPACK libraries (vecLib on MacOSX,
169	                       ATLAS elsewhere), use --link-lapack_opt.
170	                       See also --help-link switch. [NO_MESON]
171	
172	  -L/path/to/lib/ -l<libname>
173	  -D<define> -U<name>
174	  -I/path/to/include/
175	  <filename>.o <filename>.so <filename>.a
176	
177	  Using the following macros may be required with non-gcc Fortran
178	  compilers:
179	    -DPREPEND_FORTRAN -DNO_APPEND_FORTRAN -DUPPERCASE_FORTRAN
180	
181	  When using -DF2PY_REPORT_ATEXIT, a performance report of F2PY
182	  interface is printed out at exit (platforms: Linux).
183	
184	  When using -DF2PY_REPORT_ON_ARRAY_COPY=<int>, a message is
185	  sent to stderr whenever F2PY interface makes a copy of an
186	  array. Integer <int> sets the threshold for array sizes when
187	  a message should be shown.
188	
189	Version:     {f2py_version}
190	numpy Version: {numpy_version}
191	License:     NumPy license (see LICENSE.txt in the NumPy source code)
